OBJECT Report 11020203 Consolidated WIP Reporting
{
  OBJECT-PROPERTIES
  {
    Date=;
    Time=;
    Version List=4PS14.00;
  }
  PROPERTIES
  {
    CaptionML=[DEU=Konsolidierte WIP Berichtswesen;
               ENU=Consolidated Reporting Projects;
               NLD=Geconsolideerde OHW rapportage;
               NOR=Konsoliderte prosjektrapporter;
               SVE=Konsoliderade rapportering projekt];
    OnPreReport=BEGIN
                  JobsSetup.GET;

                  IF EndDate = 0D THEN
                    ERROR(Text000);
                  IF (EndDate < StartDate) THEN
                    ERROR(Text001);
                END;

  }
  DATASET
  {
    { 1100525002;;DataItem;                  ;
               DataItemTable=Table2000000026;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Number)
                                 WHERE(Number=CONST(1));
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               Job.DPA_SetFilters(CurrReport.OBJECTID(FALSE));
                             END;
                              }

    { 1100525001;1;Column;COMPANYNAME        ;
               SourceExpr=COMPANYPROPERTY.DISPLAYNAME }

    { 1100525000;1;Column;REPORTNAME         ;
               SourceExpr=GetReportName }

    { 1100525004;1;Column;REPORTFILTER       ;

    { 1100525109;1;Column;DPA_GetFiltersFltrGrp7;
               SourceExpr=Job.DPA_GetFiltersFltrGrp(7) }

    { 1100525110;1;Column;PrintDetailed      ;
               SourceExpr=PrintDetailed }

    { 1100525111;1;Column;PeriodFilter       ;
               SourceExpr=STRSUBSTNO(Text002,StartDate,EndDate) }

    { 1100525005;;DataItem;                  ;
               DataItemTable=Table11072003;
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               DPA_SetFilters(CurrReport.OBJECTID(FALSE));
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  ProjectType@1100525002 : Record 11012009;
                                  I@1100525000 : Integer;
                                BEGIN
                                  PreResultDC := 0;

                                  DetermineStockFactor;

                                  IF NOT ProjectType.GET("Project Type") THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;

                                  IF ProjectType."Method Preclosure Results" = ProjectType."Method Preclosure Results"::Net THEN
                                    PreResultDC := CalcPreclosurePerJob("No.", ProjectType."Preclosure Acc. Loss (Credit)", ProjectType."Preclosure Acc. Profit (Debit)")
                                  ELSE
                                    PreResultDC := CalcPreclosurePerJob("No.", ProjectType."Preclosure Acc. Costs (Credit)", ProjectType."Preclosure Acc. Sales (Debit)");

                                  CLEAR(ProjectDCGL);
                                  CLEAR(ProjectBCGL);
                                  CLEAR(ProjectConsGL);
                                  CLEAR(ProjectStock);
                                  CLEAR(ProjectDebet);
                                  CLEAR(ProjectCredit);

                                  CalcProjectCostsAndRevenues('', "No.");
                                  IF (JobsSetup."Company Type" <> JobsSetup."Company Type"::"Construction Company") AND
                                     ("Joint Company" <> '') AND
                                     ("Joint Job No." <> '')
                                  THEN
                                    CalcProjectCostsAndRevenues("Joint Company", "Joint Job No.");

                                  FOR I := 1 TO 7 DO
                                    ProjectConsGL[I] := ProjectDCGL[I] + ProjectBCGL[I];

                                  ProjectConsGL[6] := ProjectConsGL[1] + ProjectConsGL[2] + ProjectConsGL[3] + ProjectConsGL[4] + ProjectConsGL[5];
                                  ProjectDCGL[6] := ProjectDCGL[1] + ProjectDCGL[2] + ProjectDCGL[3] + ProjectDCGL[4] + ProjectDCGL[5];
                                  ProjectBCGL[6] := ProjectBCGL[1] + ProjectBCGL[2] + ProjectBCGL[3] + ProjectBCGL[4] + ProjectBCGL[5];

                                  FOR I := 1 TO 6 DO BEGIN
                                    ProjectStock[I] := ProjectConsGL[I] * StockFactor;
                                    IF ProjectConsGL[I] > 0 THEN
                                      ProjectDebet[I] := ProjectConsGL[I] - ProjectStock[I]
                                    ELSE
                                      ProjectCredit[I] := (ProjectConsGL[I] - ProjectStock[I]) * -1;
                                  END;

                                  IF ProjectConsGL[7] > 0 THEN
                                    ProjectCredit[7] := ProjectConsGL[7]
                                  ELSE
                                    ProjectDebet[7] := ProjectConsGL[7] * -1;

                                  // WIP Position = Total WIP Costs - Revenues
                                  ProjectConsGL[8] := ProjectConsGL[6] - ProjectConsGL[7];
                                  ProjectDCGL[8] := ProjectDCGL[6] - ProjectDCGL[7];
                                  ProjectBCGL[8] := ProjectBCGL[6] - ProjectBCGL[7];

                                  ProjectStock[8] := ProjectStock[6];
                                  IF ProjectConsGL[8] > 0 THEN
                                    ProjectDebet[8] := ProjectConsGL[8] - ProjectStock[8]
                                  ELSE
                                    ProjectCredit[8] := (ProjectConsGL[8] - ProjectStock[8]) * -1;

                                  // Pre-result
                                  ProjectConsGL[9] := PreResultDC;
                                  ProjectDCGL[9] := PreResultDC;
                                  ProjectBCGL[9] := 0;

                                  IF ProjectConsGL[9] > 0 THEN
                                    ProjectCredit[9] := ProjectConsGL[9]
                                  ELSE
                                    ProjectDebet[9] := ProjectConsGL[9] * -1;

                                  // Total WIP
                                  ProjectConsGL[10] := ProjectConsGL[8] + ProjectConsGL[9];
                                  ProjectDCGL[10] := ProjectDCGL[8] - ProjectDCGL[9];
                                  ProjectBCGL[10] := ProjectBCGL[8] - ProjectBCGL[9];

                                  ProjectStock[10] := ProjectStock[6];
                                  IF ProjectConsGL[10] > 0 THEN
                                    ProjectDebet[10] := ProjectConsGL[10] - ProjectStock[10]
                                  ELSE
                                    ProjectCredit[10] := (ProjectConsGL[10]  - ProjectStock[10]) * -1;


                                  FOR I := 1 TO 10 DO BEGIN
                                    TotalDCGL[I] := TotalDCGL[I] + ProjectDCGL[I];
                                    TotalBCGL[I] := TotalBCGL[I] + ProjectBCGL[I];
                                    TotalConsGL[I] := TotalConsGL[I] + ProjectConsGL[I];
                                    TotalStock[I] := TotalStock[I] + ProjectStock[I];
                                  END;
                                END;

               ReqFilterFields=No.,Project Type,Project Status }

    { 1100525008;1;Column;No_Job             ;
               SourceExpr=Job."No." }

    { 1100525009;1;Column;Description_Job    ;
               SourceExpr=Job.Description }

    { 1100525051;;DataItem;Total             ;
               DataItemTable=Table2000000026;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Number)
                                 WHERE(Number=CONST(1));
               OnPreDataItem=VAR
                               I@1100525000 : Integer;
                             BEGIN
                               FOR I := 1 TO 10 DO BEGIN
                                 IF (I <> 7) AND (I <> 9) THEN BEGIN
                                   IF TotalConsGL[I] > 0 THEN
                                     TotalDebet[I] := TotalConsGL[I] - TotalStock[I]
                                   ELSE
                                     TotalCredit[I] := (TotalConsGL[I] - TotalStock[I]) * -1;
                                 END ELSE BEGIN
                                   IF TotalConsGL[I] > 0 THEN
                                     TotalCredit[I] := TotalConsGL[I]
                                   ELSE
                                     TotalDebet[I] := TotalConsGL[I] * -1;
                                 END;
                               END;
                             END;
                              }

    VAR

      TotalDCGL@1100525007 : ARRAY [10] OF Decimal;
      TotalBCGL@1100525021 : ARRAY [10] OF Decimal;
      TotalConsGL@1100525020 : ARRAY [10] OF Decimal;
      TotalStock@1100525006 : ARRAY [10] OF Decimal;
      TotalDebet@1100525005 : ARRAY [10] OF Decimal;
      TotalCredit@1100525004 : ARRAY [10] OF Decimal;
      PreResultDC@1100525003 : Decimal;
      StartDate@1100525015 : Date;
      EndDate@1100525014 : Date;
      PrintDetailed@1100525013 : Boolean;
      Text000@1100525017 : TextConst 'DEU=Das Enddatum muss eingegeben werden.;ENU=End date must be filled.;NLD=Einddatum moeten worden ingevuld.;NOR=Sluttdato m† fylles ut';
      Text001@1100525016 : TextConst 'DEU=Enddatum darf nicht kleiner als das Startdatum sein.;ENU=End date may not be less than the start date.;NLD=Einddatum mag niet kleiner zijn dan de begindatum.;NOR=Sluttdato kan ikke inntreffe tidligere enn startdato;SVE=Slutdatum f†r inte infalla tidigare „n startdatum.';
      Text002@1100525002 : TextConst 'DEU=Periode: %1..%2;ENU=Period: %1..%2;NLD=Periode: %1..%2;NOR=Periode: %1..%2;SVE=Period: %1..%2';

    PROCEDURE GetReportName@1100525003() : Text;
    BEGIN
      EXIT(DELSTR(CurrReport.OBJECTID, 1, STRPOS(CurrReport.OBJECTID, ' ')));
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetReportFilter@1100525000() : Text;
    BEGIN
      IF Integer.GETFILTERS <> '' THEN
        EXIT(STRSUBSTNO('%1: %2', Integer.TABLECAPTION, Integer.GETFILTERS));
    END;

    PROCEDURE DetermineStockFactor@1100525010();
    VAR
      ProjectPreclosureResult@1100525000 : Record 11012093;
    BEGIN
      //Get Stock factor
      //It is difficult to get stockfactor from G/L, get it from Project Preclosure Results.
      //when a project is closed we assume there is no stock anymore.
      StockFactor := 0;
      IF Job."Preclosure Result" <> Job."Preclosure Result"::No THEN BEGIN
        ProjectPreclosureResult.SETCURRENTKEY("Project No.","Posting Date");
        ProjectPreclosureResult.SETRANGE("Project No.", Job."No.");
        ProjectPreclosureResult.SETFILTER("Posting Date", '>%1', EndDate);
        ProjectPreclosureResult.SETRANGE(Posted, TRUE);
        IF Job."Project Status" >= Job."Project Status"::Finished THEN
          IF NOT ProjectPreclosureResult.FINDFIRST THEN
            EXIT; //Job already is closed (we don't know when but somewhere between EndDate and TODAY) don't display a stock

        ProjectPreclosureResult.SETFILTER("Posting Date", '..%1', EndDate);
        IF ProjectPreclosureResult.FINDLAST THEN BEGIN
          IF Job."Preclosure Result" = Job."Preclosure Result"::"Sales Progress" THEN BEGIN
            IF ProjectPreclosureResult."Units Saleable" <> 0 THEN
              StockFactor := 1 - (ProjectPreclosureResult."Units Sold" / ProjectPreclosureResult."Units Saleable");
          END;
        END;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE CalcProjectCostsAndRevenues@1100525001(CompanyBC@1100525000 : Text;JobNo@1100525001 : Code[20]);
    VAR
      Job@1100525002 : Record 11072003;
      ProjectType@1100525003 : Record 11012009;
      TempGLAccount@1100528400 : TEMPORARY Record 15;
      I@1100525004 : Integer;
    BEGIN
      // Assumptions:
      //
      // The fields "WIP Account Labor", "WIP Account Material", "WIP Account Subcontracting"
      // "WIP Account Plant" and "WIP Account Sundry" of the project type are filled with different account no.'s.
      //
      // The fields "WIP Account Revenue", "WIP Account Revenue Labor", "WIP Account Revenue Material",
      // "WIP Account Revenue Subcontr.", "WIP Account Revenue Plant" and "WIP Account Revenue Sundry"
      // may be filled with the same account no., but not with one of the "cost" WIP Account no's.
      //
      // TempGLAccount is used to make sure that the amount of a G/L entry will not be multiplied
      // by the number of times the account no. occurs in the WIP Account Revenue fields of the project type.

      IF CompanyBC <> '' THEN BEGIN
        Job.CHANGECOMPANY(CompanyBC);
        ProjectType.CHANGECOMPANY(CompanyBC);
      END;

      Job.GET(JobNo);
      ProjectType.GET(Job."Project Type");

      FOR I := 1 TO 6 DO BEGIN
        CASE I OF
          1: IF ProjectType."WIP Account Labor" <> '' THEN
               CalcProjectGL(Job."No.", ProjectType."WIP Account Labor", I, CompanyBC, TempGLAccount);
          2: IF ProjectType."WIP Account Material" <> '' THEN
               CalcProjectGL(Job."No.", ProjectType."WIP Account Material", I, CompanyBC, TempGLAccount);
          3: IF ProjectType."WIP Account Subcontracting" <> '' THEN
               CalcProjectGL(Job."No.", ProjectType."WIP Account Subcontracting", I, CompanyBC, TempGLAccount);
          4: IF ProjectType."WIP Account Plant" <> '' THEN
               CalcProjectGL(Job."No.", ProjectType."WIP Account Plant", I, CompanyBC, TempGLAccount);
          5: IF ProjectType."WIP Account Sundry" <> '' THEN
               CalcProjectGL(Job."No.", ProjectType."WIP Account Sundry", I, CompanyBC, TempGLAccount);
          6: BEGIN
               IF ProjectType."WIP Account Revenue" <> '' THEN
                 CalcProjectGL(Job."No.", ProjectType."WIP Account Revenue", I, CompanyBC, TempGLAccount);
               IF ProjectType."WIP Account Revenue Labor" <> '' THEN
                 CalcProjectGL(Job."No.", ProjectType."WIP Account Revenue Labor", I, CompanyBC, TempGLAccount);
               IF ProjectType."WIP Account Revenue Material" <> '' THEN
                 CalcProjectGL(Job."No.", ProjectType."WIP Account Revenue Material", I, CompanyBC, TempGLAccount);
               IF ProjectType."WIP Account Revenue Subcontr." <> '' THEN
                 CalcProjectGL(Job."No.", ProjectType."WIP Account Revenue Subcontr.", I, CompanyBC, TempGLAccount);
               IF ProjectType."WIP Account Revenue Plant" <> '' THEN
                 CalcProjectGL(Job."No.", ProjectType."WIP Account Revenue Plant", I, CompanyBC, TempGLAccount);
               IF ProjectType."WIP Account Revenue Sundry" <> '' THEN
                 CalcProjectGL(Job."No.", ProjectType."WIP Account Revenue Sundry", I, CompanyBC, TempGLAccount);
             END;
        END;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE CalcProjectGL@1210190031(JobNo@1100525002 : Code[20];AccountNo@1210190000 : Code[20];CostType@1210190001 : ',Labor,Material,Subcontracting,Plant,Sundry,Revenues';CompanyBC@1100525001 : Text[50];VAR TempGLAccount@1100528400 : TEMPORARY Record 15);
    VAR
      GLEntry@1100525000 : Record 17;
    BEGIN
      IF TempGLAccount.GET(AccountNo) THEN
        EXIT;

      TempGLAccount."No." := AccountNo;
      TempGLAccount.INSERT;

      IF CompanyBC <> '' THEN
        GLEntry.CHANGECOMPANY(CompanyBC);

      GLEntry.SETCURRENTKEY("G/L Account No.","Posting Date");
      GLEntry.SETRANGE("G/L Account No.", AccountNo);
      GLEntry.SETFILTER("Posting Date", '%1..%2', StartDate, EndDate);
      GLEntry.SETRANGE("Job No.", JobNo);
      GLEntry.DPA_SetFilters(CurrReport.OBJECTID(FALSE));
      IF GLEntry.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
          IF CompanyBC <> '' THEN BEGIN
            IF CostType <> CostType::Revenues THEN
              ProjectBCGL[CostType] := ProjectBCGL[CostType] + GLEntry.Amount
            ELSE
              ProjectBCGL[7] := ProjectBCGL[7] + (GLEntry.Amount * -1);
          END ELSE BEGIN
            IF CostType <> CostType::Revenues THEN
              ProjectDCGL[CostType] := ProjectDCGL[CostType] + GLEntry.Amount
            ELSE
              ProjectDCGL[7] := ProjectDCGL[7] + (GLEntry.Amount * -1);
          END;
        UNTIL GLEntry.NEXT = 0;
    END;

    PROCEDURE CalcPreclosurePerJob@1100525004(JobNo@1100525002 : Code[20];CreditAccountNo@1210190000 : Code[20];DebitAccountNo@1100525000 : Code[20]) : Decimal;
    VAR
      GLEntry@1100525001 : Record 17;
      PreclosureResult@1210190002 : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      PreclosureResult := 0;

      GLEntry.SETCURRENTKEY("G/L Account No.","Posting Date");
      GLEntry.SETFILTER("G/L Account No.", '%1|%2', CreditAccountNo, DebitAccountNo);
      GLEntry.SETFILTER("Posting Date", '%1..%2', StartDate, EndDate);
      GLEntry.SETRANGE("Job No.", JobNo);
      IF GLEntry.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
          PreclosureResult := PreclosureResult + GLEntry.Amount;
        UNTIL GLEntry.NEXT = 0;

      EXIT(PreclosureResult);
    END;

    BEGIN
    END.
  }

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function
